If you go late, there is basically nothing to eat, especially fresh meat and seafood. There is basically no so-called seafood, only river fish and clams. There are few entertainment facilities, and there are only 4 KTV rooms. If you don't make an appoin**ent during holidays, you can't sing at all. There is always someone at the billiards table. Maybe it can only be played when there are not many people on weekdays. The other table tennis and fitness You can play basketball in the room; archery, go-karts and trampolines are suitable for kindergarten-age children, and older children will not be interested in them. Now let's talk about the hotel environment, which is also the biggest advantage of the hotel. It is located in a remote valley, a bit far from the Qiandao Lake Scenic Area, but close to the lake, with a good environment. You can see the Internet celebrity bridge if you stay in the hotel. The room facilities are relatively new, and there are many soft drinks and snacks provided. However, one thing is that only 8 bottles of purified water can be provided, which is a bit stingy. We booked a king-size bed room, and they upgraded us to a lake view king-size bed, which means we can see the Internet celebrity bridge in the room. The room is quite large and spacious and comfortable to live in, which must be praised. Overall, the stay is ok, the food and play are very average, and the overall experience is satisfactory!
